When the mouse is on an image, the mouse will show as a magnifier and you can adjust magnification with wheel. When the mouse is by the sides of an image, it will show as an arrow and wheel means going to neighboring images.\r\n4.\tFastest magnification experience. A click on an image will result to immediate magnification with no lag at all.
